<script>

	require(["jquery"], function ($) {
		var $shopLink = $(".shop-link");
		var req = new XMLHttpRequest();
		req.open("GET", document.location, false);
		req.send(null);
		var xRegion = req.getResponseHeader("x-region");
		var href = "";
		var regionLink = {
			us: "http://www.tennis-warehouse.com/?from=atp",
			eu: "http://www.tenniswarehouse-europe.com/?from=atp",
			au: "http://www.tennis-warehouse.com/?from=atp",
			na: "http://www.tennis-warehouse.com/?from=atp"
		}

		var chkShop = function (header) {
			if (header === null) {
				return $shopLink.attr("href", regionLink.us);
			}
			var regKey = header.toLowerCase();

			href = regionLink[regKey];
			return $shopLink.attr("href", href);
		}
		chkShop(xRegion);
	});
</script>

		function openLSHDWindow(year, wkno, eventid, tour, lang, ref_file, width, height, hasScrollBars) {
			// ADD NAME FIELD and make sure it get's focus!!!
			var theWidth = width;
			var theHeight = height;
			var scrollBars = "scrollbars";
			if (hasScrollBars == false) scrollBars = "scrollbars=0";
			if ((theWidth == "") || (theWidth == null)) theWidth = 1042;
			if ((theHeight == "") || (theHeight == null)) theHeight = 631;
			var theLeft = (screen.availWidth - theWidth) / 2;
			var theTop = (screen.availHeight - theHeight) / 2;
			var strCheckRef = escape(ref_file);

			var lsURL = "http://www.protennislive.com/LSHD/main.html?year=" + year + "&wkno=" + wkno + "&eventid=" + eventid + "&tour=" + tour + "&lang=" + lang + "&ref=" + strCheckRef;

			var popupWin = window.open(lsURL, '_' + Math.round(Math.random() * 1000000), 'top=' + theTop + ',left=' + theLeft + ',menubar=0,toolbar=0,location=0,directories=0,status=0,' + scrollBars + ',width=' + theWidth + ', height=' + theHeight);
		}
		function openLSBTFWindow(year, wkno, eventid, tour, lang, ref_file, width, height, hasScrollBars) {
			// ADD NAME FIELD and make sure it get's focus!!!
			var theWidth = width;
			var theHeight = height;
			var scrollBars = "scrollbars";
			if (hasScrollBars == false) scrollBars = "scrollbars=0";
			if ((theWidth == "") || (theWidth == null)) theWidth = 1042;
			if ((theHeight == "") || (theHeight == null)) theHeight = 631;
			var theLeft = (screen.availWidth - theWidth) / 2;
			var theTop = (screen.availHeight - theHeight) / 2;
			var strCheckRef = escape(ref_file);

			lsURL = "http://www.protennislive.com/lsbtf/main.html?year=" + year + "&wkno=" + wkno + "&eventid=" + eventid + "&tour=" + tour + "&lang=" + lang + "&ref=" + strCheckRef;

			var popupWin = window.open(lsURL, '_' + Math.round(Math.random() * 1000000), 'top=' + theTop + ',left=' + theLeft + ',menubar=0,toolbar=0,location=0,directories=0,status=0,' + scrollBars + ',width=' + theWidth + ', height=' + theHeight);
		}
